libtool: compile:  gcc -DHAVE_CONFIG_H -I. -I. -I/usr/include/freetype2 -I/usr/include/libxml2 -fopenmp -g -O2 -Wall -pthread -MT coders/coders_rle_la-rle.lo -MD -MP -MF coders/.deps/coders_rle_la-rle.Tpo -c coders/rle.c -o coders/coders_rle_la-rle.o >/dev/null 2>&1
mv -f coders/.deps/coders_rle_la-rle.Tpo coders/.deps/coders_rle_la-rle.Plo
/bin/sh ./libtool  --tag=CC   --mode=link gcc  -fopenmp -g -O2 -Wall -pthread -no-undefined -export-symbols-regex ".*" -shared -module -avoid-version  -o coders/rle.la -rpath /usr/lib/GraphicsMagick-1.3.22/modules-Q16/coders coders/coders_rle_la-rle.lo magick/libGraphicsMagick.la 
libtool: link: /usr/bin/nm -B  coders/.libs/coders_rle_la-rle.o   | sed -n -e 's/^.*[	 ]\([ABCDGIRSTW][ABCDGIRSTW]*\)[	 ][	 ]*\([_A-Za-z][_A-Za-z0-9]*\)$/\1 \2 \2/p' | sed '/ __gnu_lto/d' | /usr/bin/sed 's/.* //' | sort | uniq > coders/.libs/rle.exp
libtool: link: /usr/bin/grep -E -e ".*" "coders/.libs/rle.exp" > "coders/.libs/rle.expT"
libtool: link: mv -f "coders/.libs/rle.expT" "coders/.libs/rle.exp"
libtool: link: echo "{ global:" > coders/.libs/rle.ver
libtool: link:  cat coders/.libs/rle.exp | sed -e "s/\(.*\)/\1;/" >> coders/.libs/rle.ver
libtool: link:  echo "local: *; };" >> coders/.libs/rle.ver
libtool: link:  gcc -shared  -fPIC -DPIC  coders/.libs/coders_rle_la-rle.o   -Wl,-rpath -Wl,/tmp/graphicsmagick/src/GraphicsMagick-1.3.22/magick/.libs magick/.libs/libGraphicsMagick.so -llcms2 -lfreetype -lXext -lSM -lICE -lX11 -llzma -lbz2 -lz -lltdl -lm -lgomp -lpthread  -fopenmp -g -O2 -pthread   -fopenmp -pthread -Wl,-soname -Wl,rle.so -Wl,-version-script -Wl,coders/.libs/rle.ver -o coders/.libs/rle.so
libtool: link: ( cd "coders/.libs" && rm -f "rle.la" && ln -s "../rle.la" "rle.la" )
